7.Yulia Lyuricheva: The world is defined by a plethora of causal relationships. These causalities, however, are located at different tiers of human perception. In layman's terms, catching a glass before it touches the floor does not mean the glass wouldn't break within next few minutes.

9.Yulia Lyuricheva: She lives in a mansion that once belonged to a family of exiles whose political views led them to a far out town like ours.
